<h1>The Numbers - Movies Released in 2010</h1>
<center>
<div>
<a href="/movies/">&larr; Back to Movie Archive</a>
</div>
</center>
<BR>This list shows all films released in 2010, including films that went direct-to-video, or only got an international theatrical release. For each film, we use the first date on which it was made available to the public, which might include international theatrical or domestic video releases that were a few days, or sometimes more, earlier than the domestic (US/Canada) theatrical release.
<BR>The revenue listed is the worldwide box office combined with the domestic home market revenue to date.<BR><BR>See also: <a href="/box-office-records/worldwide/all-movies/cumulative/released-in-2010">Top 2010 Worldwide</a> - <a href="/movies/release-schedule/2010">Domestic Release Schedule for 2010</a> - <a href="/home-market/release-schedule/2010">Domestic Home Market Release Schedule for 2010</a> - <a href="/movies/most-popular/2010">Most Popular 2010</a><center>
<br>
